<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Military">Military</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=South_Georgia_and_the_South_Sandwich_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Military">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Royal_Navy_Antarctic_Patrol_Ship_HMS_Protector_MOD_45153156.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f1/Royal_Navy_Antarctic_Patrol_Ship_HMS_Protector_MOD_45153156.jpg/220px-Royal_Navy_Antarctic_Patrol_Ship_HMS_Protector_MOD_45153156.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f1/Royal_Navy_Antarctic_Patrol_Ship_HMS_Protector_MOD_45153156.jpg/330px-Royal_Navy_Antarctic_Patrol_Ship_HMS_Protector_MOD_45153156.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f1/Royal_Navy_Antarctic_Patrol_Ship_HMS_Protector_MOD_45153156.jpg/440px-Royal_Navy_Antarctic_Patrol_Ship_HMS_Protector_MOD_45153156.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2708" data-file-height="1807" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Royal_Navy_Antarctic_Patrol_Ship_HMS_Protector_MOD_45153156.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>HMS <i>Protector</i></div></div></div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Military_of_the_Falkland_Islands" title="Military of the Falkland Islands">Military of the Falkland Islands</a></div>
<p>After the <a href="/wiki/Falklands_War" title="Falklands War">Falklands War</a> in 1982, a full-time British military presence was maintained at <a href="/wiki/King_Edward_Point" title="King Edward Point">King Edward Point</a> on South Georgia. This was scaled down during the 1990s until the last detachment left South Georgia in March 2001, after a new station had been built and occupied by the <a href="/wiki/British_Antarctic_Survey" title="British Antarctic Survey">British Antarctic Survey</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The main British military facility in the region is at <a href="/wiki/RAF_Mount_Pleasant" title="RAF Mount Pleasant">RAF Mount Pleasant</a> and the adjacent <a href="/wiki/Mare_Harbour" title="Mare Harbour">Mare Harbour</a> naval base on <a href="/wiki/East_Falkland" title="East Falkland">East Falkland</a>, and three <a href="/wiki/Remote_Radar_Head" class="mw-redirect" title="Remote Radar Head">Remote Radar Heads</a> on the Falklands: <a href="/wiki/RRH_Mount_Kent" class="mw-redirect" title="RRH Mount Kent">RRH Mount Kent</a>, <a href="/wiki/RRH_Byron_Heights" class="mw-redirect" title="RRH Byron Heights">RRH Byron Heights</a> and <a href="/wiki/RRH_Mount_Alice" class="mw-redirect" title="RRH Mount Alice">RRH Mount Alice</a>. A handful of British naval vessels patrol the region, visiting South Georgia a few times each year and sometimes deploying small infantry patrols. Flights by RAF <a href="/wiki/C-130_Hercules" class="mw-redirect" title="C-130 Hercules">C-130 Hercules</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vickers_VC10" title="Vickers VC10">Vickers VC10</a> (replaced by Voyager) aircraft also occasionally patrol the territory.
</p><p>A Royal Navy destroyer or frigate and a <a href="/wiki/Royal_Fleet_Auxiliary" title="Royal Fleet Auxiliary">Royal Fleet Auxiliary</a> vessel carry out the <a href="/wiki/Standing_Royal_Navy_deployments" title="Standing Royal Navy deployments">Atlantic Patrol Task (South)</a> mission in the surrounding area.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/HMS_Endurance_(A171)" title="HMS Endurance (A171)">HMS&#160;<i>Endurance</i></a>, the Royal Navy ice-patrol ship, operated in the South Georgia area during part of most southern summer seasons until her near loss due to flooding in 2008. She carried out hydrological and mapping work as well as assisting with scientific fieldwork for the British Antarctic Survey, film and photographic units, and youth expedition group <a href="/wiki/BSES_Expeditions" class="mw-redirect" title="BSES Expeditions">BSES Expeditions</a>. While the final decision on the fate of <i>Endurance</i> was pending, the Royal Navy chartered a Norwegian icebreaker, renamed <a href="/wiki/HMS_Protector_(A173)" title="HMS Protector (A173)">HMS&#160;<i>Protector</i></a>, to act as replacement for three years.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> In September 2013 the British <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Defence_(United_Kingdom)" title="Ministry of Defence (United Kingdom)">Ministry of Defence</a> purchased the ship outright.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> It was announced on 7 October 2013 that <i>Endurance</i> would be sold for scrap.<sup id="cite_ref-BBC_scrapped_58-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC_scrapped-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="References">References</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=South_Georgia_and_the_South_Sandwich_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: References">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

</div></td><td class="navbox-image" rowspan="1" style="width:1px;padding:0px 0px 0px 2px"><div><a href="/wiki/File:Proposed_flag_of_Antarctica_(Graham_Bartram).svg" class="image" title="Flag of Antarctica"><img alt="Flag of Antarctica" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/Proposed_flag_of_Antarctica_%28Graham_Bartram%29.svg/64px-Proposed_flag_of_Antarctica_%28Graham_Bartram%29.svg.png" decoding="async" width="64" height="43" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/Proposed_flag_of_Antarctica_%28Graham_Bartram%29.svg/96px-Proposed_flag_of_Antarctica_%28Graham_Bartram%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/Proposed_flag_of_Antarctica_%28Graham_Bartram%29.svg/128px-Proposed_flag_of_Antarctica_%28Graham_Bartram%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="744" data-file-height="496" /></a></div></td></tr><tr><td class="navbox-abovebelow" colspan="3"><div>"Peri-Antarctic" (meaning "close to the Antarctic") does <i><b>not</b></i> include <a href="/wiki/Territorial_claims_in_Antarctica" title="Territorial claims in Antarctica">territorial claims in Antarctica itself</a>.</div></td></tr></tbody></table></div>
